		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td valign="top">
				9.
			</td>
			<td>
				The system will automatically resize your image to fit the width of the image block.
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td valign="top">
				10.
			</td>
			<td>
				To adjust the image height, go to the bottom of the image until you see the grabbers.
				Pull the grabber with your mouse up or down until your image is adjusted properly.
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td colspan="2" align="center">
				<img src="/Images/HelpImages/imgResize.jpg" />
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td valign="top">
			</td>
			<td>
				Note: The system will not allow you to make the image <u>wider</u> than the image
				block.
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td valign="top">
				11.
			</td>
			<td>
				If you would like to save the adjusted image, check the box under ‘Insert’ by image modification
				<img src="/Images/HelpImages/SaveImageCheckbox.jpg" />
				in step 5.
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td valign="top">
				12.
			</td>
			<td>
				Choose the alignment of your image by selecting from the drop down box in step 3.
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td colspan="2" align="center">
				<img src="/Images/HelpImages/ChooseAlign.jpg" />
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td valign="top">
				13.
			</td>
			<td>
				To hyperlink your image, see <a href="javascript:ModalHelpPopup(''Create Link to Image'',171,'''');" style="color:blue;">Create Link to Image</a> under Content
				Input in the Help Menu.
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td valign="top" style="padding-top:8px">
				14.
			</td>
			<td>
				When finished select ‘Insert’ in step 5.
				<img src="/Images/HelpImages/Insert.jpg" /> and your image will appear in the block.
			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>'
Where Help_ID = 194
